THE ORDEAL of RICHARD FEVEREL 



 by George Meredith 


 CHAPTER I 

 some year ago a book be publish under the title of " The Pilgrim 's Scrip . " it consist of a selection of original aphorism by an anonymous gentleman , who in this bashful manner give a bruised heart to the world . 
 he make no pretension to novelty . " our new thought have thrill dead bosom , " he write ; by which avowal it may be see that youth have manifestly go from he , since he have cease to be jealous of the ancient . there be a half - sigh float through his page for those day of intellectual coxcombry , when idea come to we affect the embrace of virgin , and swear to we they be our alone , and no one else have they ever visit : and we believe they . 
 for an example of his idea of the sex he say : 
 " I expect that Woman will be the last thing civilize by Man . " 
 some excitement be produce in the bosom of lady by so monstrous a scorn of they . 
 one adventurous person betake herself to the Heralds ' College , and there ascertain that a Griffin between two Wheatsheaves , which stand on the title - page of the book , form the crest of Sir Austin Absworthy Bearne Feverel , Baronet , of Raynham Abbey , in a certain western county fold Thames : a man of wealth and honour , and a somewhat lamentable history . 
 the outline of the baronet 's story be by no mean new . he have a wife , and he have a friend . his marriage be for love ; his wife be a beauty ; his friend be a sort of poet . his wife have his whole heart , and his friend all his confidence . when he select Denzil Somers from among his college chum , it be not on account of any similarity of disposition between they , but from his intense worship of genius , which make he overlook the absence of principle in his associate for the sake of such brilliant promise . Denzil have a small patrimony to lead off with , and that he dissipate before he leave college ; thenceforth he be dependent upon his admirer , with whom he live , fill a nominal post of bailiff to the estate , and launch forth verse of some satiric and sentimental quality ; for be incline to vice , and occasionally , and in a quiet way , practise it , he be of course a sentimentalist and a satirist , entitle to lash the age and complain of human nature . his early poem , publish under the pseudonym of Diaper Sandoe , be so pure and bloodless in their love passage , and at the same time so bite in their moral tone , that his reputation be great among the virtuous , who form the large portion of the English book - buying public . election - season call he to ballad - poetry on behalf of the Tory party . Dialer possess undoubted fluency , but do tittle , though Sir Austin be ever expect much of he . 
 a languish , inexperienced woman , whose husband in mental and in moral stature be more than the ordinary height above she , and who , now that her first romantic admiration of his lofty bearing have wear off , and her fretful little refinement of taste and sentiment be not instinctively respond to , be throw into no wholesome household collision with a fluent man , fluent in prose and rhyme . Lady Feverel , when she first enter on her duty at Raynham , be jealous of her husband 's friend . by degree she tolerate he . in time he touch his guitar in her chamber , and they play Rizzio and Mary together . 
  " for I be not the first who find 
  the name of Mary fatal ! " 
 say a subsequent sentimental alliterative love - poem of Diaper 's . 
 such be the outline of the story . but the baronet could fill it up . he have open his soul to these two . he have be noble love to the one , and to the other perfect Friendship . he have bid they be brother and sister whom he love , and live a Golden Age with he at Raynham . in fact , he have be prodigal of the excellence of his nature , which it be not good to be , and , like Timon , he become bankrupt , and fall upon bitterness . 
 the faithless lady be of no particular family ; an orphan daughter of an admiral who educate she on his half - pay , and her conduct strike but at the man whose name she bore . 
 after five year of marriage , and twelve of friendship , Sir Austin be leave to his loneliness with nothing to ease his heart of love upon save a little baby boy in a cradle . he forgive the man : he put he aside as poor for his wrath . the woman he could not forgive ; she have sin every way . simple ingratitude to a benefactor be a pardonable transgression , for he be not one to recount and crush the culprit under the heap of his good deed . but she he have raise to be his equal , and he judge she as his equal . she have blacken the world 's fair aspect for he . 
 in the presence of that world , so different to he now , he preserve his wonte demeanor , and make his feature a flexible mask . Mrs. Doria Forey , his widow sister , say that Austin might have retire from his parliamentary career for a time , and give up gaiety and that kind of thing ; her opinion , found on observation of he in public and private , be , that the light thing who have take flight be but a feather on her brother 's Feverel - heart , and his ordinary course of life would be resume . there be time when common man can not bear the weight of just so much . Hippias Feverel , one of his brother , think he immensely improve by his misfortune , if the loss of such a person could be so designated ; and see that Hippias receive in consequence free quarter at Raynham , and possession of the wing of the Abbey she have inhabit , it be profitable to know his thought . if the baronet have give two or three blaze dinner in the great hall he would have deceive people generally , as he do his relative and intimate . he be too sick for that : fit only for passive acting . 
 the nursemaid wake in the night beheld a solitary figure darken a lamp above her little sleeping charge , and become so used to the sight as never to wake with a start . one night she be strangely arouse by a sound of sobbing . the baronet stand beside the cot in his long black cloak and travel cap . his finger shade a lamp , and redden against the fitful darkness that ever and anon go leap up the wall . she could hardly believe her sens to see the austere gentleman , dead silent , drop tear upon tear before her eye . she lie stone - still in a trance of terror and mournfulness , mechanically count the tear as they fall , one by one . the hidden face , the fall and flash of those heavy drop in the light of the lamp he hold , the upright , awful figure , agitated at regular interval like a piece of clockwork by the low murderous catch of his breath : it be so piteous to her poor human nature that her heart begin wildly palpitate . involuntarily the poor girl cry out to he , " oh , sir ! " and fall a - weeping . Sir Austin turn the lamp on her pillow , and harshly bid she go to sleep , stride from the room forthwith . he dismiss she with a purse the next day . 
 once , when he be seven year old , the little fellow wake up at night to see a lady bend over he . he talk of this the neat day , but it be treat as a dream ; until in the course of the day his uncle Algernon be drive home from Lobourne cricket - ground with a broken leg . then it be recollect that there be a family ghost ; and , though no member of the family believe in the ghost , none would have give up a circumstance that testify to its existence ; for to possess a ghost be a distinction above title . 
 Algernon Feverel lose his leg , and cease to be a gentleman in the Guards . of the other uncle of young Richard , Cuthbert , the sailor , perish in a spirited boat expedition against a slaving negro chief up the Niger . some of the gallant lieutenant 's trophy of war decorate the little boy 's play - shed at Raynham , and he bequeath his sword to Richard , whose hero he be . the diplomatist and beau , Vivian , end his fluttering from flower to flower by make an improper marriage , as be the fate of many a beau , and be strike out of the list of visitor . Algernon generally occupy the baronet 's disused town - house , a wretched being , divide his time between horse and card exercise : possess , it be say , of the absurd notion that a man who have lose his balance by lose his leg may regain it by stick to the bottle . at least , whenever he and his brother Hippias get together , they never fail to try whether one leg , or two , stand the bottle well . much of a puritan as Sir Austin be in his habit , he be too good a host , and too thorough a gentleman , to impose they upon his guest . the brother , and other relative , might do as they would while they do not disgrace the name , and then it be final : they must depart to behold his countenance no more . 
 Algernon Feverel be a simple man , who feel , subsequent to his misfortune , as he have perhaps dimly fancy it before , that his career lie in his leg , and be now irrevocably cut short . he teach the boy boxing , and shooting , and the art of fence , and superintend the direction of his animal vigour with a melancholy vivacity . the remain energy of Algernon 's mind be devoted to animadversion on swift bowling . he preach it over the county , struggle through laborious literary composition , address to sporting newspaper , on the Decline of Cricket . it be Algernon who witness and chronicle young Richard 's first fight , which be with young Tom Blaize of Belthorpe Farm , three year the boy 's senior . 
 Hippias Feverel be once think to be the genius of the family . it be his ill luck to have strong appetite and a weak stomach ; and , as one be not altogether fit for the battle of life who be engage in a perpetual contention with his dinner , Hippias forsook his prospect at the Bar , and , in the embrace of dyspepsia , compile his ponderous work on the Fairy Mythology of Europe . he have little to do with the Hope of Raynham beyond what he endure from his juvenile trick . 
 a venerable lady , know as Great - Aunt Grantley , who have money to bequeath to the heir , occupy with Hippias the background of the house and share her candle with he . these two be seldom see till the dinner hour , for which they be all day prepare , and probably all night remembering , for the Eighteenth Century be an admirable trencherman , and cast age aside while there be a dish on the table . 
 Mrs. Doris Foray be the eld of the three sister of the baronet , a florid affable woman , with fine tooth , exceedingly fine light wavy hair , a Norman nose , and a reputation for understand man ; and that , with these practical creature , always mean the art of manage they . she have marry an expectant young son of a good family , who decease before the fulfilment of his prospect ; and , cast about in her mind the future chance of her little daughter and sole child , Clare , she mark down a probability . the far sight , the deep determination , the resolute perseverance of her sex , where a daughter be to be provide for and a man to be overthrow , instigate she to invite herself to Raynham , where , with that daughter , she fix herself . 
 the other two Feverel lady be the wife of Colonel Wentworth and the widow of Mr. Justice Harley : and the only thing remarkable about they be that they be mother of son of some distinction . 
 Austin Wentworth 's story be of that wretched character which to be comprehend , that justice should be deal he , must be tell out and openly ; which no one dare now do . 
 for a fault in early youth , redeem by he nobly , accord to his light , he be condemn to undergo the world 's harsh judgment : not for the fault for its atonement . 
 " marry his mother 's housemaid , " whisper Mrs. Doria , with a ghastly look , and a shudder at young man of republican sentiment , which he be repute to entertain . " ' the compensation for injustice , ' say the ' Pilgrim 's scrip , ' be , that in that dark Ordeal we gather the worthy around we . " 
 and the baronet 's fair friend , Lady Blandish , and some few true man and woman , hold Austin Wentworth high . 
 he do not live with his wife ; and Sir Austin , whose mind be bent on the future of our specie , reproach he with be barren to posterity , while knave be propagate . 
 the principal characteristic of the second nephew , Adrian Harley , be his sagacity . he be essentially the wise youth , both in counsel and in action . 
 " in action , " the " Pilgrim 's Scrip " observe , " wisdom go by majority . " 
 Adrian have an instinct for the majority , and , as the world invariably find he enlisted in its rank , his appellation of wise youth be acquiesce in without irony . 
 the wise youth , then , have the world with he , but no friend . nor do he wish for those troublesome appendage of success . he cause himself to be require by people who could serve he ; fear by such as could injure . not that he go out of the way to secure his end , or risk the expense of a plot . he do the work as easily as he eat his daily bread . Adrian be an epicurean ; one whom Epicurus would have scourge out of his garden , certainly : an epicurean of our modern notion . to satisfy his appetite without rashly stake his character , be the wise youth 's problem for life . he have no intimate except Gibbon and Horace , and the society of these fine aristocrat of literature help he to accept humanity as it have be , and be ; a supreme ironic procession , with laughter of Gods in the background . why not laughter of mortal also ? Adrian have his laugh in his comfortable corner . he possess peculiar attribute of a heathen God . he be a disposer of man : he be polished , luxurious , and happy at their cost . he live in eminent self - content , as one lie on soft cloud , lapt in sunshine . nor Jove , nor Apollo , cast eye upon the maid of earth with cooler fire of selection , or pursue they in the covert with more sacred impunity . and he enjoy his reputation for virtue as something additional . steal fruit be say to be sweet ; undeserved reward be exquisite . 
 the good of it be , that Adrian make no pretence . he do not solicit the favourable judgment of the world . nature and he attempt no other concealment than the ordinary mask man wear . and yet the world would proclaim he moral , as well as wise , and the pleasing converse every way of his disgrace cousin Austin . 
 in a word , Adrian Harley have master his philosophy at the early age of one - and - twenty . many would be glad to say the same at that age twice - tell : they carry in their breast a burden with which Adrian 's be not load . Mrs. Doria be nearly right about his heart . a singular mishap   at his birth , possibly , or before it   have unseat that organ , and shake it down to his stomach , where it be a much light , nay , an inspire weight , and encourage he merrily onward . throne there it look on little that do not arrive to gratify it . already that region be a trifle prominent in the person of the wise youth , and carry , as it be , the flag of his philosophical tenet in front of he . he be charming after dinner , with man or with woman : delightfully sarcastic : perhaps a little too unscrupulous in his moral tone , but that his moral reputation belie he , and it must be set down to generosity of disposition . 
 such be Adrian Harley , another of Sir Austin 's intellectual favourite , choose from mankind to superintend the education of his son at Raynham . Adrian have be destine for the Church . he do not enter into order . he and the baronet have a conference together one day , and from that time Adrian become a fixture in the Abbey . his father die in his promising son 's college term , bequeath he nothing but his legal complexion , and Adrian become stipendiary officer in his uncle 's household . 
 a playfellow of Richard 's occasionally , and the only comrade of his age that he ever see , be Master Ripton Thompson , the son of Sir Austin 's solicitor , a boy without a character . 
 a comrade of some description be necessary , for Richard be neither to go to school nor to college . Sir Austin consider that the school be corrupt , and maintain that young lad might by parental vigilance be keep pretty secure from the Serpent until Eve side with he : a period that might be defer , he say . he have a system of education for his son . how it work we shall see . 




 CHAPTER II 

 October , shine royally on Richard 's fourteenth birthday . the brown beechwood and golden birch glow to a brilliant sun . bank of moveless cloud hang about the horizon , mound to the west , where sleep the wind . promise of a great day for Raynham , as it prove to be , though not in the manner mark out . 
 already archery - booth and cricketing - tent be rise on the low ground towards the river , whither the lad of Bursley and Lobourne , in boat and in cart , shout for a day of ale and honour , jogged merrily to match themselves anew , and pluck at the lining laurel from each other 's brow , line manly Britons . the whole park be begin to be astir and resound with holiday cry . Sir Austin Feverel , a thorough good Tory , be no game - preserver , and could be popular whenever he choose , which Sir Males Papworth , on the other side of the river , a fast - handed Whig and terror to poacher , never could be . half the village of Lobourne be see troop through the avenue of the park . fiddler and gipsy clamour at the gate for admission : white smock , and slate , surmount by hat of serious brim , and now and then a scarlet cloak , smacking of the old country , dot the grassy sweep to the level . 
 and all the time the star of these festivity be recede far and far , and eclipse himself with his reluctant serf Ripton , who keep ask what they be to do and where they be go , and how late it be in the day , and suggest that the lad of Lobourne would be call out for they , and Sir Austin require their presence , without get any attention pay to his misery or remonstrance . for Richard have be request by his father to submit to medical examination like a boor enlisting for a soldier , and he be in great wrath . 
 he be fly as though he would have fly from the shameful thought of what have be ask of he . by - and - by he communicate his sentiment to Ripton , who say they be those of a girl : an offensive remark , remember which , Richard , after they have borrow a couple of gun at the bailiff 's farm , and Ripton have fire badly , call his friend a fool . 
 feel that circumstance be make he look wonderfully like one , Ripton lift his head and retort defiantly , " I be not ! " 
 this angry contradiction , so very uncalled for , annoyed Richard , who be still smart at the loss of the bird , owe to Ripton 's bad shot , and be really the injure party . he , therefore bestow the abusive epithet on Ripton anew , and with increase of emphasis . 
 " you shall not   call I so , then , whether I be or not , " say Ripton , and suck his lip . 
 this be become personal . Richard send up his brow , and star at his defier an instant . he then inform he that he certainly should call he so , and would not object to call he so twenty time . 
 " do it , and see ! " return Ripton , rock on his foot , and breathe quick . 
 with a gravity of which only boy and other barbarian be capable , Richard go through the entire number , stress the epithet to increase the defiance and avoid monotony , as he progress , while Ripton bob his head every time in assent , as it be , to his comrade 's accuracy , and as a record for his profound humiliation . the dog they have with they gaze at the extraordinary performance with interrogating wag of the tail . 
 twenty time , duly and deliberately , Richard repeat the obnoxious word . 
 at the twentieth solemn iteration of Ripton 's capital shortcoming , Ripton deliver a smart back - hander on Richard 's mouth , and square precipitately ; perhaps sorry when the deed be do , for he be a kind - hearted lad , and as Richard simply bow in acknowledgment of the blow he think he have go too far . he do not know the young gentleman he be deal with . Richard be extremely cool . 
 " shall we fight here ? " he say . 
 " anywhere you like , " reply Ripton . 
 " a little more into the wood , I think . we may be interrupt . " and Richard lead the way with a courteous reserve that somewhat chill Ripton 's ardour for the contest . on the skirt of the wood , Richard throw off his jacket and waistcoat , and , quite collect , wait for Ripton to do the same . the latter boy be flushed and restless ; old and broad , but not so tight - limbed and well - set . the Gods , sole witness of their battle , bet dead against he . Richard have mount the white cockade of the Feverels , and there be a look in he that ask for tough work to extinguish . his brow , slightly line upward at the temple , converge to a knot about the well - set straight nose ; his full grey eye , open nostril , and plant foot , and a gentlemanly air of calm and alertness , form a spirited picture of a young combatant . as for Ripton , he be all abroad , and fight in school - boy style that be , he rush at the foe head foremost , and strike like a windmill . he be a lumpy boy . when he do hit , he make himself feel ; but he be at the mercy of science . to see he come dash in , blink and puff and whirl his arm abroad while the felling blow go straight between they , you perceive that he be fight a fight of desperation , and know it . for the dreaded alternative glare he in the face that , if he yield , he must look like what he have be twenty time calumniously call ; and he would die rather than yield , and swing his windmill till he drop . poor boy ! he drop frequently . the gallant fellow fight for appearance , and down he go . the Gods favour one of two party . Prince Turnus be a noble youth ; but he have not Pallas at his elbow . Ripton be a capital boy ; he have no science . he could not prove he be not a fool ! when one come to think of it , Ripton do choose the only possible way , and we should all of we have considerable difficulty in prove the negative by any other . Ripton come on the unerre fist again and again ; and if it be true , as he say in short colloquial gasp , that he require as much beat as an egg to be beat thoroughly , a fortunate interruption alone save our friend from resemble that substance . the boy hear summon voice , and beheld Mr. Morton of Poer Hall and Austin Wentworth step towards they . 
 a truce be sound , jacket be catch up , gun shoulder , and off they trot in concert through the depth of the wood , not stop till that and half - a - dozen field and a larch plantation be well behind they . 
 when they halt to take breath , there be a mutual study of face . Ripton 's be much discolour , and look fiercer with its natural war - paint than the boy feel . nevertheless , he square up dauntlessly on the new ground , and Richard , whose wrath be appease , could not refrain from ask he whether he have not really have enough . 
 " never ! " shout the noble enemy . 
 " well , look here , " say Richard , appeal to common sense , " I be tired of knock you down . I will say you be not a fool , if you will give I your hand . " 
 Ripton demur an instant to consult with honour , who bid he catch at his chance . 
 he hold out his hand . " there ! " and the boy grasp hand and be fast friend . Ripton have gain his point , and Richard decidedly have the good of it . so , they be on equal ground . both , could claim a victory , which be all the well for their friendship . 
 Ripton wash his face and comfort his nose at a brook , and be now ready to follow his friend wherever he choose to lead . they continue to beat about for bird . the bird on the Raynham estate be find singularly cunning , and repeatedly elude the aim of these prime shot , so they push their expedition into the land of their neighbor , in search of a stupider race , happily oblivious of the law and condition of trespass ; unconscious , too , that they be poach on the demesne of the notorious Farmer Blaize , the free - trade farmer under the shield of the Papworths , no worshipper of the Griffin between two Wheatsheaves ; destine to be much ally with Richard 's fortune from begin to end . Farmer Blaize hat poacher , and , especially young chap poach , who do it mostly from impudence . he hear the audacious shot pop right and leave , and go forth to have a glimpse at the intruder , and observe their size , swear he would teach my gentleman a thing , lord or no lord . 
 Richard have bring down a beautiful cock - pheasant , and be exult over it , when the farmer 's portentous figure burst upon they , crack an avenge horsewhip . his salute be ironical . 
 " havin' good sport , gentleman , be ye ? " 
 " just bag a splendid bird ! " radiant Richard inform he . 
 " oh ! " Farmer Blaize give an admonitory flick of the whip . 
 " just let I clap eye on't , then . " 
 " say , please , " interpose Ripton , who be not blind to doubtful aspect . 
 Farmer Blaize throw up his chin , and grin grimly . 
 " please to you , sir ? why , my chap , you look as if ye do not   much mind what come t'yer nose , I reckon . you look an old poacher , you do . tall ye what ' tis ' ! " he change his banter to business , " that bird 's mine ! now you jest hand he over , and sheer off , you dam young scoundrel ! I know ye ! " and he become exceedingly opprobrious , and utter contempt of the name of Feverel . 
 Richard open his eye . 
 " if you want to be horsewhip , you will stay where y'are ! " continue the farmer . " Giles Blaize never stand nonsense ! " 
 " then we will stay , " quoth Richard . 
 " good ! so be't ! if you will have't , have't , my man ! " 
 as a preparatory measure , Farmer Blaize seize a wing of the bird , on which both boy fling themselves desperately , and secure it minus the pinion . 
 " that be your game , " cry the farmer . " here be a taste of horsewhip for ye . I never stand nonsense ! " and sweetch go the mighty whip , well sway . the boy try to close with he . he keep his distance and lash without mercy . black blood be make by Farmer Blaize that day ! the boy wriggle , in spite of themselves . it be like a relentless serpent coiling , and bite , and sting their young vein to madness . probably they feel the disgrace of the contortion they be make to go through more than the pain , but the pain be fierce , for the farmer lay about from a practised arm , and do not consider that he have do enough till he be well breathe and his ruddy jowl inflame . he pause , to receive the remainder of the cock - pheasant in his face . 
 " take your beastly bird , " cry Richard . 
 " Money , my lad , and interest , " roar the farmer , lash out again . 
 shameful as it be to retreat , there be but that course open to they . they decide to surrender the field . 
 " look ! you big brute , " Richard shake his gun , hoarse with passion , " I would have shoot you , if I have be load . mind if I come across you when I be load , you coward , I will fire ! " the un - english nature of this threat exasperate Farmer Blaize , and he press the pursuit in time to bestow a few farewell stripe as they be escape tight - breeched into neutral territory . at the hedge they parley a minute , the farmer to inquire if they have have a mortal good tanning and be satisfied , for when they want a further instalment of the same they be to come for it to Belthorpe Farm , and there it be in pickle : the boy meantime explode in menace and threat of vengeance , on which the farmer contemptuously turn his back . Ripton have already stock an armful of flint for the enjoyment of a little skirmishing . Richard , however , knock they all out , say , " no ! gentleman do not   fle stone ; leave that to the blackguard . " 
 " just one shy at he ! " plead Ripton , with his eye on Farmer Blaize 's broad mark , and his whole mind drunken with a sudden revelation of the advantage of light troop in opposition to heavy . 
 " no , " say Richard , imperatively , " no stone , " and march briskly away . Ripton follow with a sigh . his leader 's magnanimity be wholly beyond he . a good spanking mark at the farmer would have relieve Master Ripton ; it would have do nothing to console Richard Feverel for the ignominy he have be compel to submit to . Ripton be familiar with the rod , a monster much despoiled of his terror by intimacy . birch - fever be past with this boy . the horrible sense of shame , self - loathing , universal hatred , impotent vengeance , as if the spirit be steep in abysmal blackness , which come upon a courageous and sensitive youth condemn for the first time to taste this piece of fleshly bitterness , and suffer what he feel be a defilement , Ripton have weather and forget . he be seasoned wood , and take the world pretty wisely ; not reckless of castigation , as some boy become , nor oversensitive as to dishonour , as his friend and comrade beside he be . 
 Richard 's blood be poison . he have the fever on he severely . he would not allow stone - flinging , because it be a habit of his to discountenance it . mere gentlemanly consideration have scarce shield Farmer Blaize , and certain very ungentlemanly scheme be come to ghastly head in the tumult of his brain ; reject solely from their glare impracticability even to his young intelligence . a sweeping and consummate vengeance for the indignity alone should satisfy he . something tremendous must be do ; and do without delay . at one moment he think of kill all the farmer 's cattle ; next of kill he ; challenge he to single combat with the arm , and accord to the fashion of gentleman . but the farmer be a coward ; he would refuse . then he , Richard Feverel , would stand by the farmer 's bedside , and rouse he ; rouse he to fight with powder and ball in his own chamber , in the cowardly midnight , where he might tremble , but dare not refuse . 
 " Lord ! " cry simple Ripton , while these hopeful plot be rag in his comrade 's brain , now sparkle for immediate execution , and anon lapsing disdainfully dark in their chance of fulfilment , " how I wish you would have let I notch he , Ricky ! I be a safe shot . I never miss . I should feel quite jolly if I have spank he once . we should have have the beat of he at that game . I say ! " and a sharp thought draw Ripton 's idea nearer home , " I wonder whether my nose be as bad as he say ! where can I see myself ? " 
 to these exclamation Richard be deaf , and he trudge steadily forward , face but one object . 
 after tear through innumerable hedge , leap fence , jump dyke , penetrate brambly copse , and get dirty , ragged , and tired , Ripton awake from his dream of Farmer Blaize and a blue nose to the vivid consciousness of hunger ; and this grow with the rapidity of light upon he , till in the course of another minute he be endure the extreme of famine , and venture to question his leader whither he be be conduct . Raynham be out of sight . they be a long way down the valley , mile from Lobourne , in a country of sour pool , yellow brook , rank pasturage , desolate heath . solitary cow be see ; the smoke of a mud cottage ; a cart pile with peat ; a donkey graze at leisure , oblivious of an unkind world ; geese by a horse - pond , gabble as in the first loneliness of creation ; uncooked thing that a famishing boy can not possibly care for , and must despise . Ripton be in despair . 
 " where be you go to ? " he inquire with a voice of the last time of ask , and halt resolutely . 
 Richard now break his silence to reply , " anywhere . " 
 " anywhere ! " Ripton take up the moody word . " but be not   you awfully hungry ? " he gasp vehemently , in a way that show the total emptiness of his stomach . 
 " no , " be Richard 's brief response . 
 " not hungry ! " Ripton 's amazement lend he increase vehemence . " why , you have not   have anything to eat since breakfast ! not hungry ? I declare I be starve . I feel such a gnawing I could eat dry bread and cheese ! " 
 Richard sneer : not for reason that would have actuate a similar demonstration of the philosopher . 
 " come , " cry Ripton , " at all event , tell we where you be go to stop . " 
 Richard face about to make a querulous retort . the injured and hapless visage that meet his eye disarm he . the lad 's nose , though not exactly of the dread hue , be really become discolour . to upbraid he would be cruel . Richard lift his head , survey the position , and exclaim " here ! " drop down on a withered bank , leave Ripton to contemplate he as a puzzle whose every new move be a bad perplexity . 




 CHAPTER III 

 among boy there be law of honour and chivalrous code , not write or formally teach , but intuitively understand by all , and invariably act upon by the loyal and the true . the race be not nearly civilized , we must remember . thus , not to follow your leader whithersoever he may think proper to lead ; to back out of an expedition because the end of it frown dubious , and the present fruit of it be discomfort ; to quit a comrade on the road , and return home without he : these be trick which no boy of spirit would be guilty of , let he come to any description of mortal grief in consequence . well so than have his own conscience denounce he sneak . some boy who behave boldly enough be not trouble by this conscience , and the eye and the lip of their fellow have to supply the deficiency . they do it with just as haunting , and even more horrible pertinacity , than the inner voice , and the result , if the probation be not very severe and searching , be the same . the leader can rely on the faithfulness of his host : the comrade be swear to serve . Master Ripton Thompson be naturally loyal . the idea of turn off and forsake his friend never once cross his mind , though his condition be desperate , and his friend 's behaviour that of a Bedlamite . he announce several time impatiently that they would be too late for dinner . his friend do not budge . " in some country , I hear , they manage their good sport at night - time , and beat up for game with torch . it must be a fine sight . after all , the country would be dull if we have not   a rip here and there to treat we to a little conflagration .  CHAPTER VI 

 as soon as they could escape , the boy get together into an obscure corner of the park , and there take counsel of their extremity .

 CHAPTER VII 

 a little laurel - shade temple of white marble look out on the river from a knoll border the Raynham beechwood , and be dub by Adrian Daphne 's Bower . to this spot Richard have retire , and there Austin find he with his head bury in his hand , a picture of desperation , whose last shift have be defeat . he allow Austin to greet he and sit by he without lift his head . perhaps his eye be not presentable .

"

 CHAPTER VIII

 CHAPTER X 

 to have determine upon an act something akin to heroism in its way , and to have fulfil it by lie heartily , and so subvert the whole structure build by good resolution , seem a sad downfall if we forget what human nature , in its green weedy spring , be compose of .  CHAPTER XI 

 of all the chief actor in the Bakewell Comedy , Master Ripton Thompson await the fearful morning which be to decide Tom 's fate , in dolefull mood , and suffer the grave mental terror .  in the paternal home , under the roof of Law , and remove from the influence of his conscienceless young chief , the staggering nature of the act he have put his hand to , its awful felonious aspect , overwhelmed Ripton . he see it now for the first time .  " Dear Ripton , if Tom have be commit I would have shoot old Blaize . do you know my father be behind we that night when Clare see the ghost and hear all we say before the fire burst out . it be no use try to conceal anything from he . well as you be in an awful state I will tell you all about it . after you leave Ripton I have a conversation with Austin and he persuade I to go down to old Blaize and ask he to help off Tom .  poor little Letitia , after three perusal of this ingenuous epistle , where the law of punctuation be so disregarded , resign it to one of the pocket of her brother Ripton 's good jacket , deeply smite with the careless composer . and so end the last act of the Bakewell Comedy , in which the curtain close with Sir Austin 's point out to his friend the beneficial action of the System in it from begin to end . 




 CHAPTER XII 

 Laying of ghost be a public duty , and , as the mystery of the apparition that have frighten little Clare be never solve on the stage of event at Raynham , where dread walk the Abbey , let we go behind the scene a moment . morally superstitious as the baronet be , the character of his mind be oppose to anything like spiritual agency in the affair of man , and , when the matter be make clear to he , it shake off a weight of weakness and restore his mental balance ; so that from this time he go about more like the man he have once be , grasp more thoroughly the great truth , that this World be well design .  far behind the scene we observe Rizzio and Mary grow old , much disenchanted : she discrowne , dishevel , he with gouty finger on a greasy guitar . the Diaper Sandoe of promise lend his pen for small hire . his fame have sink ; his bodily girth have sensibly increase . what he can do , and will do , be still his theme ; meantime the juice of the juniper be in requisition , and it seem that those small hire can not be perform without it . return from her wretched journey to her wretcheder home , the lady have to listen to a mild reproof from easy - go diaper , a reproof so mild that he couch it in blank verse : for , seldom write metrically now , he take to talk it . with a fluent sympathetic tear , he explain to she that she be damage her interest by these proceeding ; nor do he shrink from undertaking to elucidate wherefore . plume a smile upon his succulent mouth , he tell she that the poverty she live in be utterly unbefitte her gentle nurture , and that he have reason to believe could assure she that an annuity be on the point of be grant she by her husband . and Diaper break his bud of a smile into full flower as he deliver this information . she learn that he have apply to her husband for money . it be hard to have one 's prop of self - respect cut away just when we be suffer a martyr 's agony at the stake . there be a five minute ' tragic colloquy in the recess behind the scene , totally tragic to Diaper , who have fondly hop to bask in the warm sun of that annuity , and re - emerge from his state of grub . the lady then write the letter Sir Austin hold open to his sister . the atmosphere behind the scene be not wholesome , so , have lay the Ghost , we will return and face the curtain . 
 that infinitesimal dose of the World which Master Ripton Thompson have furnish to the System with such instantaneous and surprising effect be consider by Sir Austin to have work well , and to be for the time quite sufficient , so that Ripton do not receive a second invitation to Raynham , and Richard have no special intimate of his own age to rub his excessive vitality against , and want none . his hand be full enough with Tom Bakewell . moreover , his father and he be heart in heart . the boy 's mind be open , and turn to his father affectionately reverent . at this period , when the young savage grow into high influence , the faculty of worship be foremost in he . at this period Jesuits will stamp the future of their chargeling flock ; and all who bring up youth by a System , and watch it , know that it be the malleable moment . boy possess any mental or moral force to give they a tendency , then predestinate their career ; or , if under supervision , take the impress that be give they : not often to cast it off , and seldom to cast it off altogether . 
 in Sir Austin 's note - book be write : " between simple Boyhood and Adolescence the Blossoming Season on the threshold of Puberty , there be one Unselfish Hour say , Spiritual seed - time . " 
 he take care that good seed should be plant in Richard , and that the most fruitful seed for a youth , namely , Example , should be of a kind to germinate in he the love of every form of nobleness . 
 " I be only strive to make my son a Christian , " he say , answer they who persist in expostulate with the System . and to these instruction he give an aim : " first be virtuous , " he tell his son , " and then serve your country with heart and soul . " the youth be instruct to cherish an ambition for statesmanship , and he and his father read history and the speech of british orator to some purpose ; for one day Sir Austin find he lean cross - legged , and with his hand to his chin , against a pedestal support the bust of Chatham , contemplate the hero of our Parliament , his eye stream with tear . 
 People say the baronet carry the principle of Example so far that he only retain his boozing dyspeptic brother Hippias at Raynham in order to exhibit to his son the woeful retribution nature wreak upon a life of indulgence ; poor Hippias have now become a walking complaint . this be unjust , but there be no doubt he make use of every illustration to disgust or encourage his son that his neighbourhood afford he , and do not spare his brother , for whom Richard entertain a contempt in proportion to his admiration of his father , and be for fly into penitential extreme which Sir Austin have to soften .

 CHAPTER XIV

 CHAPTER XIX 

 away with Systems ! away with a corrupt world ! let we breathe the air of the Enchanted Island . 
 golden lie the meadow : golden run the stream ; red gold be on the pine - stem . the sun be come down to earth , and walk the field and the water . 
 the sun be come down to earth , and the field and the water shout to he golden shout . he come , and his herald run before he , and touch the leaf of oak and plane and beeche lucid green , and the pine - stem redder gold ; leave bright footprint upon thickly - weed bank , where the foxglove 's last upper - bell incline , and bramble - shoot wander amid moist rich herbage . the plume of the woodland be alight ; and beyond they , over the open , ' tis a race with the long - throw shadow ; a race across the heath and up the hill , till , at the farth bourne of mount eastern cloud , the herald of the sun lie rosy finger and rest . 
 Sweet be the shy recess of the woodland . the ray tread softly there . a film athwart the pathway quiver many - hue against purple shade fragrant with warm pine , deep moss - bed , feathery fern . the little brown squirrel drop tail , and leap ; the inmost bird be startled to a chance tuneless note . from silence into silence thing move . 
 Peeps of the revel splendour above and around enliven the conscious full heart within . the flaming West , the crimson height , shower their glory through voluminous leafage . but these be bower where deep bliss dwell , imperial joy , that owe no fealty to yonder glory , in which the young lamb gambol and the spirit of man be glad . descend , great Radiance ! embrace creation with beneficent fire , and pass from we ! you and the vice - regal light that succeed to you , and all heavenly pageant , be the minister and the slave of the throb content within . 
 for this be the home of the enchantment . here , seclude from vex shore , the prince and princess of the island meet : here like darkle nightingale they sit , and into eye and ear and hand pour endless ever - fresh treasure of their soul . 
 roll on , grind wheel of the world : cry of ship go down in a calm , groan of a system which will not know its rightful hour of exultation , complain to the universe . you be not hear here . 
 he call she by her name , Lucy : and she , blush at her great boldness , have call he by his , Richard . those two name be the key - note of the wonderful harmony the angel sing aloft . 
 " Lucy ! my beloved ! " 
 " o Richard ! " 
 out in the world there , on the skirt of the woodland , a sheep - boy pipe to meditative eve on a penny - whistle .

 now surely there will come an age when the presentation of science at war with Fortune and the Fates , will be deem the true epic of modern life ; and the aspect of a scientific humanist who , by dint of incessant watchfulness , have maintain a system against those active forty , can not be reckon less than sublime , even though at the moment he but sit upon his horse , on a fine March morning such as this , and smile wistfully to behold the son of his heart , his system incarnate , wave a serene adieu to tutelage , neither too eager nor morbidly unwilling to try his luck alone for a term of two week . at present , I be aware , an audience impatient for blood and glory scorn the stress I be put on incident so minute , a picture so little impose . an audience will come to whom it will be give to see the elementary machinery at work : who , as it be , from some slight hint of the straw , will feel the wind of March when they do not blow . to they will nothing be trivial , see that they will have in their eye the invisible conflict go on around we , whose feature a nod , a smile , a laugh of ours perpetually change . and they will perceive , moreover , that in real life all hang together : the train be lay in the lifting of an eyebrow , that burst upon the field of thousand . they will see the link of thing as they pass , and wonder not , as foolish people now do , that this great matter come out of that small one .

 CHAPTER XXIX 

 although it blow hard when Caesar cross the Rubicon , the passage of that river be commonly calm ; calm as Acheron . so long as he get his fare , the ferryman do not need to be tell whom he carry : he pull with a will , and hero may be over in half - an - hour . only when they stand on the opposite bank , do they see what a leap they have take . the shore they have relinquish shrink to an infinite remoteness . there they have dream : here they must act . there lie youth and irresolution : here manhood and purpose . they be veritably in another land : a moral Acheron divide their life . their memory scarce seem their own ! the Philosophical Geography   about to be publish   observe that each man have , one time or other , a little Rubicon a clear or a foul water to cross . it be ask he : " wilt thou we d this fate , and give up all behind thee ? " and " I will , " firmly pronounce , speed he over . the above - name manuscript authority inform we , that by far the great number of caress roll by this heroic flood to its sister stream below , be those of fellow who have repent their pledge , and have try to swim back to the bank they have blot out . for though every man of we may be a hero for one fatal minute , very few remain so after a day 's march even : and who wonder that Madam Fate be indignant , and wear the feature of the terrible Universal Fate to he ? fail before she , either in heart or in act , and lo , how the alluring love in her visage wither and sicken to what it be model on ! be your Rubicon big or small , clear or foul , it be the same : you shall not return . on or to Acheron ! I subscribe to that saying of the Pilgrim 's scrip : 
 " the danger of a little knowledge of thing be disputable : but beware the little knowledge of one 's self ! " 
 Richard Feverel be now cross the River of his Ordeal . already the mist be steal over the land he have leave : his life be cut in two , and he breathe but the air that meet his nostril . his father , his father 's love , his boyhood and ambition , be shadowy . his poetic dream have take a live attainable shape . he have a distincter impression of the Autumnal Berry and her household than of anything at Raynham . and yet the young man love his father , love his home : and I daresay Caesar love Rome : but whether he do or no , Caesar when he kill the Republic be quite bald , and the hero we be deal with be scarce begin to feel his despotic moustache . do he know what he be make of ? Doubtless , nothing at all . but honest passion have an instinct that can be safe than conscious wisdom . he be an arrow draw to the head , fly from the bow . his audacious mendacity and subterfuge do not strike he as in any way criminal ; for he be perfectly sure that the winning and securing of Lucy would in the end be boisterously approve of , and in that case , be not the mean justify ? not that he take trouble to argue thus , as old hero and self - convict villain be in the habit of do ; to deduce a clear conscience . Conscience and Lucy go together . 
 it be a soft fair day . the Rubicon sparkle in the morning sun . one of those day when London embrace the prospect of summer , and troop forth all its baby . the pavement , the square , the park , be early alive with the cry of young Britain . Violet and primrose girl , and organ boy with military monkey , and systematic band very determined in tone if not in tune , fill the atmosphere , and crown the blaze procession of omnibus , freight with business man , Cityward , where a column of reddish brown smoke , blow aloft by the South - west , mark the scene of conflict to which these persistent warrior repair .  CHAPTER XXX 

 and the next moment the bride be weep as if she would dissolve to one of Dian 's Virgin Fountains from the clasp of the Sun - God . she have nobly preserve the mask impose by comedy , till the curtain have fall , and now she weep , stream with tear . have patience , o impetuous young man ! it be your profession to be a hero . this poor heart be new to it , and her duty involve such wild act , such brigandage , such terror and task , she be quite unnerved . she do you honour till now .  say : be it not enough to cause feminine apprehension , for a woman to be marry in another woman 's ring ?

 CHAPTER XXXIII 

 and now the author of the System be on trial under the eye of the lady who love he . what so kind as they ? yet be they very rigorous , those soft watchful woman 's eye . if you be below the measure they have make of you , you will feel it in the fulness of time . she can not but show you that she take you for a giant , and have have to come down a bit . you feel yourself strangely diminish in those sweet mirror , till at last they drop on you complacently level . but , oh beware , vain man , of ever wax enamour of that wonderful elongation of a male creature you see reflect in her adore upcast orb ! beware of assist to delude she ! a woman who be not quite a fool will forgive your being but a man , if you be surely that : she will haply learn to acknowledge that no mortal tailor could have fit that figure she make of you respectably , and that practically   though she sigh to think it   her ideal of you be on the pattern of an overgrown charity - boy in the regulation jacket and breech . for this she first scorn the narrow capacity of the tailor , and then smile at herself . but shouldst thou , when the hour say plainly , be thyself , and the woman be willing to take thee as thou art , shouldst thou still aspire to be that thing of shank and wrest , wilt thou not seem contemptible as well as ridiculous ? and when the fall come , will it not be flat on thy face , instead of to the common height of man ? you may fall mile below her measure of you , and be safe : nothing be damage save an overgrown charity - boy ; but if you fall below the common height of man , you must make up your mind to see her rustle her gown , spy at the look - glass , and transfer her allegiance . the moral of which be , that if we pretend to be what we be not , woman , for whose amusement the farce be perform , will find we out and punish we for it . and it be usually the end of a sentimental dalliance .

 CHAPTER XXXVII 

 Behold the hero embark in the redemption of an err beautiful woman . 

 " alas ! " write the Pilgrim at this very time to Lady Blandish , " I can not get that legend of the Serpent from I , the more I think . have he not catch you , and rank you foremost in his legion ? for see : till you be fashion , the fruit hang immobile on the bough . they sway before we , glisten and cold . the hand must be eager that pluck they . they do not come down to we , and smile , and speak our language , and read our thought , and know when to fly , when to follow ! how surely to have we ! 
 " do but mark one of you stand openly in the track of the Serpent . what shall be do with she ? " 
 this alliterative production be write without any sense of the peril that make prophecy .

 CHAPTER XXXVIII 

 one may suppose that a prematurely aged , oily little man ; a poet in bad circumstance ; a decrepit butterfly chain to a disappointed inkstand , will not put out strenuous energy to retain his ancient paramour when a robust young man come imperatively to demand his mother of he in her person . the colloquy be short between Diaper Sandoe and Richard . the question be refer to the poor spiritless lady , who , see that her son make no question of it , cast herself on his hand . small loss to she be diaper ; but he be the loss of habit , and that be something to a woman who have live . the blood of her son have be run so long alien from she that the sense of her motherhood smite he now with strangeness , and Richard 's stern gentleness seem like dreadful justice come upon she . her heart have almost forget its maternal function . she call he Sir , till he bid she remember he be her son . her voice sound to he like that of a break - throate lamb , so painful and weak it be , with the plaintive stop in the utterance . when he kiss she , her skin be cold . her thin hand fall out of his when his grasp relate . " can sin hunt one like this ? " he ask , bitterly reproach himself for the shame she have cause he to endure , and a deep compassion fill his breast . 
 poetic justice have be deal to Diaper the poet . he think of all he have sacrifice for this woman the comfortable quarter , the friend , the happy flight . he could not but accuse she of unfaithfulness in leave he in his old age . Habit have legalize his union with she . he write as pathetically of the break of habit as man feel at the death of love , and when we be old and have no fair hope toss golden lock before we , a wound to this our second nature be quite as sad . I know not even if it be not actually sad . 
 day by day Richard visit his mother . Lady Blandish and Ripton alone be in the secret . Adrian let he do as he please . he think proper to tell he that the public recognition he accord to a particular lady be , in the present state of the world , scarcely prudent . 
 " ' tis a proof to I of your moral rectitude , my son , but the world will not think so . no one character be sufficient to cover two in a protestant country especially . the divinity that doth hedge a Bishop would have no chance , in contact with your Madam Danae . drop the woman , my son . or permit I to speak what you would have her hear . " 
 Richard listen to he with disgust . " well , you have   have my doctorial warning , " say Adrian ; and plunge back into his book . 
 when Lady Feverel have revive to take part in the consultation Mrs. Berry perpetually open on the subject of Richard 's matrimonial duty , another chain be cast about he . " do not , oh , do not offend your father ! " be her one repeat supplication . Sir Austin have grow to be a vindictive phantom in her mind . she never weep but when she say this . 
 so Mrs. Berry , to whom Richard have once make mention of Lady Blandish as the only friend he have among woman , bundle off in her black - satin dress to obtain an interview with she , and an ally . after come to an understanding on the matter of the visit , and reiterate many of her view concern young married people , Mrs. Berry say : " my lady , if I may speak so bold , I would say the sin that be bein ' do be the sin o ' the looker - on . and when everybody appear frightened by that young gentleman 's father , I will say hopin ' your pardon they no cause be fright at all . for though it be nigh twenty year since I know he , and I know he then just sixteen month no more I will say his heart 's as soft as a woman 's , which I have   cause for to know . and that be it . that be where everybody be deceive by he , and I be . it be because he keep his face , and make ye think you be dealin ' with a man of iron , and all the while there be a woman underneath . and a man that be like a woman he be the puzzle o ' life ! we can see through ourselves , my lady , and we can see through man , but one o ' that sort he be like something out of nature . then I say hopin ' be excuse what be to do be for to treat he like a woman , and not for to let he have his own way which he do not   know himself , and be why nobody else do . let that sweet young couple come together , and be wholesome in spite of he , I say ; and then give he time to come round , just like a woman ; and round he will come , and give them his blessin ' , and we shall know we have   make he comfortable . he be angry because matrimony have come between he and his son , and he , woman - like , he be wantin ' to treat what be as if it be not . but matrimony be a holier than he . it begin long long before he , and it be be hop will endoor long the time after , if the world be not come to rack wishin ' he no harm . " 
 now Mrs. Berry only put Lady Blandish 's thought in bad English . the lady take upon herself seriously to advise Richard to send for his wife . he write , bid she come . Lucy , however , have wit , and inexperienced wit be as a little knowledge . in pursuance of her sage plan to make the family feel her worth , and to conquer the member of it one by one , she have get up a correspondence with Adrian , whom it tickle . Adrian constantly assure she all be go well : time would heal the wound if both the offender have the fortitude to be patient : he fancy he see sign of the baronet 's relenting : they must do nothing to arrest those favourable symptom . indeed the wise youth be languidly seek to produce they . he write , and feel , as Lucy 's benefactor . so Lucy reply to her husband a cheerful rigmarole he could make nothing of , save that she be happy in hope , and still have fear . then Mrs. Berry train her fist to indite a letter to her bride . her bride answer it by say she trust to time . " you poor marter " Mrs. Berry write back , " I know what your sufferin 's be . they be the only kind a wife should never hide from her husband . he think all sort of thing if she can abide be away . and you trust to time , why it be like trust not to catch cold out of your natural clothe . " there be no shake Lucy 's firmness . 
 Richard give it up . he begin to think that the life lie behind he be the life of a fool . what have he do in it ? he have burn a rick and get marry ! he associate the two act of his existence . where be the hero he be to have carve out of Tom Bakewell ! a wretch he have teach to lie and chicane : and for what ? great heaven ! how ignoble do a flash from the light of his aspiration make his marriage appear ! the young man seek amusement . he allow his aunt to drag he into society , and sick of that he make late evening call on Mrs. Mount , oblivious of the purpose he have in visit she at all . her man - like conversation , which he take for honesty , be a refreshing change on fair lip . 
 " call I Bella : I will call you Dick , " say she . and it come to be Bella and Dick between they . no mention of Bella occur in Richard 's letter to Lucy . 
 Mrs. Mount speak quite openly of herself . " I pretend to be no well than I be , " she say , " and I know I be no bad than many a woman who hold her head high . " to back this she tell he story of bloom dame of good repute , and pour a little social sewerage into his ear . 
 also she understand he . " what you want , my dear Dick , be something to do . you go and get marry like a hum ! friend must be respectful . go into the Army . try the turf . I can put you up to a trick or two friend should make themselves useful . " 
 she tell he what she like in he . " you be the only man I be ever alone with who do not   talk to I of love and make I feel sick . I hate man who can not   speak to a woman sensibly . just wait a minute . " she leave he and presently return with , " ah , Dick ! old fellow ! how be you ? " array like a cavalier , one arm stick in her side , her hat jauntily cock , and a pretty oath on her lip to give reality to the costume . " what do you think of I ? be not   it a shame to make a woman of I when I be bear to be a man ? " 
 " I do not   know that , " say Richard , for the contrast in her attire to those shoot eye and lip , air her sex bewitchingly . 
 " what ! you think I do not   do it well ? " 
 " Charming ! but I can not   forget ... " 
 " now that be too bad ! " she pout . 
 then she propose that they should go out into the midnight street arm - in - arm , and out they go and have great fit of laughter at her impertinent manner of use her eyeglass , and outrageous affectation of the supreme dandy . 
 " they take up man , Dick , for go about in woman 's clothe , and vice versaw , I suppose . you will bail I , old fellaa , if I have to make my bow to the beak , will not   you ? say it be beca I be an honest woman and do not   care to hide the a unmentionable when I wear they as the t'other do , " sprinkle with the dandy 's famous invocation . 
 he begin to conceive romance in that sort of fun . 
 " you be a wopper , my brave Dick ! will not   let any peel take I ? by Jove ! " 
 and he with many assurance guarantee to stand by she , while she bend her thin finger try the muscle of his arm ; and repose upon it more . there be delicacy in her dandyism . she be a graceful cavalier . 
 " Sir Julius , " as they name the dandy 's attire , be frequently call for on his evening visit to Mrs. Mount . when he behold Sir Julius he think of the lady , and " vice versaw , " as Sir Julius be fond of exclaim . 
 be ever hero in this fashion woo ? 
 the woman now and then would peep through Sir Julius . or she would sit , and talk , and altogether forget she be impersonate that worthy fop . 
 she never utter an idea or a reflection , but Richard think she the clever woman he have ever meet . 
 all kind of problematic notion beset he . she be cold as ice , she hat talk about love , and she be brand by the world .

 Sir Austin Feverel have come to town with the serenity of a philosopher who say , ' tis now time ; and the satisfaction of a man who have not arrive thereat without a struggle . he have almost forgive his son . his deep love for he have well - nigh shake loose from wounded pride and more tenacious vanity . stirring of a remote sympathy for the creature who have rob he of his son and hew at his system , be in his heart of heart . this he know ; and in his own mind he take credit for his softness . but the world must not suppose he soft ; the world must think he be still act on his system . otherwise what would his long absence signify ? something highly unphilosophical . so , though love be strong , and be move he to a straightforward course , the last tug of vanity draw he still aslant .
