 he hold she two hand that she might look on he and not spare the horrible wound he be go to lay open to her eye . 
 " Lucy . do you know why I come to you to - night ? " 
 she move her lip repeat his word . 
 " Lucy . have you guess why I do not come before ? " 
 her head shake widened eye . 
 " Lucy . I do not come because I be not worthy of my wife ! do you understand ? " 
 " darling , " she falter plaintively , and hang crouch under he , " what have I do to make you angry with I ? " 
 " o beloved ! " cry he , the tear burst out of his eye . " o beloved ! " be all he could say , kiss her hand passionately . 
 she wait , reassure , but in terror . 
 " Lucy . I stay away from you I could not come to you , because ... I dare not come to you , my wife , my beloved ! I could not come because I be a coward : because hear I this be the reason : I have break my marriage oath . " 
 again her lip move . she catch at a dim fleshless mean in they . " but you love I ? Richard ! my husband ! you love I ? " 
 " yes . I have never love , I never shall love , woman but you . " 
 " Darling ! kiss I . " 
 " have you understand what I have tell you ? " 
 " kiss I , " she say . 
 he do not join lip . " I have come to you to - night to ask your forgiveness . " 
 her answer be : " kiss I . " 
 " can you forgive a man so base ? " 
 " but you love I , Richard ? " 
 " yes : that I can say before God . I love you , and I have betray you , and be unworthy of you not worthy to touch your hand , to kneel at your foot , to breathe the same air with you . " 
 her eye shine brilliantly . " you love I ! you love I , darling ! " and as one who have sail through dark fear into daylight , she say : " my husband ! my darling ! you will never leave I ? we never shall be part again ? " 
 he draw his breath painfully . to smooth her face grow rigid with fresh fear at his silence , he meet her mouth . that kiss in which she speak what her soul have to say , calm she , and she smile happily from it , and in her manner remind he of his first vision of she on the summer morning in the field of the meadow - sweet . he hold she to he , and think then of a holier picture : of Mother and child : of the sweet wonder of life she have make real to he . 
 have he not absolve his conscience ? at least the pang to come make he think so . he now follow her lead hand . Lucy whisper : " you must not   disturb he must not   touch he , dear ! " and with dainty finger draw off the covering to the little shoulder . one arm of the child be out along the pillow ; the small hand open . his baby - mouth be pout full ; the dark lash of his eye seem to lie on his plump cheek . Richard stoop lower down to he , hunger for some movement as a sign that he live . Lucy whisper . " he sleep like you , Richard one arm under his head . " great wonder , and the stir of a grasp tenderness be in Richard . he breathe quick and soft , bend lower , till Lucy 's curl , as she nestle and bend with he , roll on the crimson quilt of the cot . a smile go up the plump cheek : forthwith the bud of a mouth be in rapid motion . the young mother whisper , blush : " he be dream of I , " and the simple word do more than Richard 's eye to make he see what be . then Lucy begin to hum and buzz sweet baby - language , and some of the tiny finger stir , and he make as if to change his cosy position , but reconsider , and defer it , with a peaceful little sigh . Lucy whisper : " he be such a big fellow . oh ! when you see he awake he be so like you , Richard . " 
 he do not hear she immediately : it seem a bit of heaven drop there in his likeness : the more human the fact of the child grow the more heavenly it seem . his son ! his child ! should he ever see he awake ? at the thought , he take the word that have be speak , and start from the dream he have be in . " will he wake soon , Lucy ? " 
 " oh no ! not yet , dear : not for hour . I would have keep he awake for you , but he be so sleepy . " 
 Richard stand back from the cot . he think that if he see the eye of his boy , and have he once on his heart , he never should have force to leave he . then he look down on he , again struggle to tear himself away . two nature war in his bosom , or it may have be the magian Conflict still go on . he have come to see his child once and to make peace with his wife before it should be too late . might he not stop with they ? might he not relinquish that devilish pledge ? be not divine happiness here offer to he ? if foolish Ripton have not delay to tell he of his interview with Mountfalcon all might have be well . but pride say it be impossible . and then injury speak . for why be he thus base and spot to the darling of his love ? a mad pleasure in the prospect of wreak vengeance on the villain who have lay the trap for he , once more blacken his brain . if he would stay he could not . so he resolve , throw the burden on Fate . the struggle be over , but oh , the pain ! 
 Lucy behold the tear stream hot from his face on the child 's cot . she marvel at such excess of emotion . but when his chest heave , and the extremity of mortal anguish appear to have seize he , her heart sink , and she try to get he in her arm . he turn away from she and go to the window . a half - moon be over the lake . 
 " look ! " he say , " do you remember our rowing there one night , and we see the shadow of the cypress ? I wish I could have come early to - night that we might have have another row , and I have hear you sing there ! " 
 " Darling ! " say she , " will it make you happy if I go with you now ? I will . " 
 " no , Lucy . Lucy , you be brave ! " 
 " oh , no ! that I be not . I think so once . I know I be not now . " 
 " yes ! to have live the child on your heart and never to have utter a complaint ! you be brave . o my Lucy ! my wife ! you that have make I man ! I call you a coward . I remember it . I be the coward I the wretched vain fool ! darling ! I be go to leave you now . you be brave , and you will bear it . listen : in two day , or three , I may be back back for good , if you will accept I . promise I to go to bed quietly . kiss the child for I , and tell he his father have see he . he will learn to speak soon . will he soon speak , Lucy ? " 
 dreadful suspicion keep she speechless ; she could only clutch one arm of his with both her hand . 
 " go ? " she presently gasp . 
 " for two or three day . no more I hope . " 
 " to - night ? " 
 " yes . now . " 
 " go now ? my husband ! " her faculty abandon she . 
 " you will be brave , my Lucy ! " 
 " Richard ! my darling husband ! go ? what be it take you from I ? " but question no far , she fall on her knee , and cry piteously to he to stay not to leave they . then she drag he to the little sleeper , and urge he to pray by his side , and he do , but rise abruptly from his prayer when he have mutter a few break word she pray on with tight - string nerve , in the faith that what she say to the interceding Mother above would be strong than human hand on he . nor could he go while she kneel there . 
 and he waver . he have not reckon on her terrible suffering . she come to he , quiet . " I know you would remain . " and take his hand , innocently fondle it : " be I so changed from she he love ? you will not leave I , dear ? " but dread return , and the word quaver as she speak they . 
 he be almost vanquish by the loveliness of her womanhood . she draw his hand to her heart , and strain it there under one breast . " come : lie on my heart , " she murmur with a smile of holy sweetness . 
 he waver more , and droop to she , but summon the power of hell , kiss she suddenly , cry the word of parting , and hurry to the door . it be over in an instant . she cry out his name , cling to he wildly , and be adjure to be brave , for he would be dishonour if he do not go . then she be shake off . 
 Mrs. Berry be arouse by an unusual prolong wailing of the child , which show that no one be comfort it , and fail to get any answer to her application for admittance , she make bold to enter . there she see Lucy , the child in her lap , sit on the floor senseless : she have take it from its sleep and try to follow her husband with it as her strong appeal to he , and have faint . 
 " oh my ! oh my ! " Mrs. Berry moan , " and I just now thinkin ' they be so happy ! " 
 Warming and caress the poor infant , she manage by degree to revive Lucy , and hear what have bring she to that situation . 
 " go to his father , " say Mrs. Berry . " Ta - te - tiddle - te - heighty - o ! go , my love , and every horse in Raynham shall be out after ' m. this be what man bring we to ! Heighty - oighty - iddlety - ah ! or you take blessed baby , and I will go . " 
 the baronet himself knock at the door . " what be this ? " he say . " I hear a noise and a step descend . " 
 " it be Mr. Richard have go , Sir Austin ! have go from his wife and babe ! Rum - te - um - te - iddledy Oh , my goodness ! what sorrow be come on we ! " and Mrs. Berry weep , and sing to baby , and baby cry vehemently , and Lucy , sobbing , take he and dance he and sing to he with draw lip and tear drop over he . and if the scientific Humanist to the day of his death forget the sight of those two poor true woman jig on their wretched heart to calm the child , he must have very little of the human in he . 
 there be no more sleep for Raynham that night . 




 CHAPTER XLV 

 " his ordeal be over . I have just come from his room and see he bear the bad that could be . return at once he have ask for you . I can hardly write intelligibly , but I will tell you what we know . 
 " two day after the dreadful night when he leave we , his father hear from Ralph Morton . Richard have fight a duel in France with Lord Mountfalcon , and be lie wound at a hamlet on the coast . his father start immediately with his poor wife , and I follow in company with his aunt and his child . the wound be not dangerous . he be shoot in the side somewhere , but the ball injure no vital part . we think all would be well . oh ! how sick I be of theory , and Systems , and the pretension of man ! there be his son lie all but dead , and the man be still unconvinced of the folly he have be guilty of . I could hardly bear the sight of his composure . I shall hate the name of Science till the day I die . give I nothing but commonplace unpretende people ! 
 " they be at a wretched french cabaret , smell vilely , where we still remain , and the people try as much as they can do to compensate for our discomfort by their kindness . the french poor people be very considerate where they see suffering . I will say that for they . the doctor have not allow his poor Lucy to go near he . she sit outside his door , and none of we dare disturb she . that be a sight for Science . his father and myself , and Mrs. Berry , be the only one permit to wait on he , and whenever we come out , there she sit , not speak a word for she have be tell it would endanger his life but she look such awful eagerness . she have the sort of eye I fancy mad person have . I be sure her reason be go . we do everything we could think of to comfort she . a bed be make up for she and her meal be bring to she there . of course there be no get she to eat . what do you suppose his alarm be fix on ? he absolutely say to I but I have not patience to repeat his word . he think she to blame for not command herself for the sake of her maternal duty . he have absolutely an idea of insist that she should make an effort to suckle the child . I shall love that Mrs. Berry to the end of my day . I really believe she have twice the sense of any of we Science and all . she ask he plainly if he wish to poison the child , and then he give way , but with a bad grace . 
 " poor man ! perhaps I be hard on he . I remember that you say Richard have do wrong . yes ; well , that may be . but his father eclipse his wrong in a great wrong a crime , or quite as bad ; for if he deceive himself in the belief that he be act righteously in separate husband and wife , and expose his son as he do , I can only say that there be some who be bad than people who deliberately commit crime . no doubt Science will benefit by it . they kill little animal for the sake of Science . 
 " we have with we Doctor Bairam , and a french physician from Dieppe , a very skilful man . it be he who tell we where the real danger lie . we think all would be well . a week have pass , and no fever supervene . we tell Richard that his wife be come to he , and he could bear to hear it . I go to she and begin to circumlocute , think she listen she have the same eager look . when I tell she she might go in with I to see her dear husband , her feature do not change . M. Despres , who hold her pulse at the time , tell I , in a whisper , it be cerebral fever brain fever come on . we have talk of she since . I notice that though she do not seem to understand I , her bosom heave , and she appear to be try to repress it , and choke something . I be sure now , from what I know of her character , that she even in the approach of delirium be prevent herself from cry out . her last hold of reason be a thought for Richard . it be against a creature like this that we plot ! I have the comfort of know that I do my share in help to destroy she . have she see her husband a day or two before but no ! there be a new system to interdict that ! or have she not so violently control her nature as she do , I believe she might have be save . 
 " he say once of a man , that his conscience be a coxcomb . will you believe that when he see his son 's wife poor victim ! lie delirious , he could not even then see his error . you say he wish to take Providence out of God 's hand . his mad self - deceit would not leave he . I be positive , that while he be stand over she , he be blame she for not have consider the child . indeed he make a remark to I that it be unfortunate ' disastrous , ' I think he say that the child should have to be feed by hand . I dare say it be . all I pray be that this young child may be save from he . I can not bear to see he look on it . he do not spare himself bodily fatigue but what be that ? that be the vulgar form of love . I know what you will say . you will say I have lose all charity , and I have . but I should not feel so , Austin , if I could be quite sure that he be an altered man even now the blow have strike he . he be reserve and simple in his speech , and his grief be evident , but I have doubt . he hear she while she be senseless call he cruel and harsh , and cry that she have suffer , and I see then his mouth contract as if he have be touch . perhaps , when he think , his mind will be clear , but what he have do can not be undo . I do not imagine he will abuse woman any more . the doctor call she a ' forte et belle jeune femme : ' and he say she be as noble a soul as ever God mould clay upon . a noble soul ' forte et belle ! ' she lie upstairs . if he can look on she and not see his sin , I almost fear God will never enlighten he . " 
 she die five day after she have be remove . the shock have utterly derange she . I be with she . she die very quietly , breathe her last breath without pain ask for no one a death I should like to die . 
 " her cry at one time be dreadfully loud . she scream that she be ' drown in fire , ' and that her husband would not come to she to save she . we deaden the sound as much as we could , but it be impossible to prevent Richard from hear . he know her voice , and it produce an effect like fever on he . whenever she call he answer . you could not hear they without weep . Mrs. Berry sit with she , and I sit with he , and his father move from one to the other . 
 " but the trial for we come when she be go . how to communicate it to Richard or whether to do so at all ! his father consult with we . we be quite decide that it would be madness to breathe it while he be in that state . I can admit now as thing have turn out we be wrong . his father leave we I believe he spend the time in prayer and then lean on I , he go to Richard , and say in so many word , that his Lucy be no more . I think it must kill he . he listen , and smile . I never see a smile so sweet and so sad . he say he have see she die , as if he have pass through his suffering a long time ago . he shut his eye . I could see by the motion of his eyeball up that he be strain his sight to some inner heaven . I can not go on . 
 " I think Richard be safe . have we postpone the tiding , till he come to his clear sens , it must have kill he . his father be right for once , then . but if he have save his son 's body , he have give the death - blow to his heart . Richard will never be what he promise . 
 " a letter find on his clothe tell we the origin of the quarrel . I have have an interview with Lord M. this morning . I can not say I think he exactly to blame : Richard force he to fight . at least I do not select he the foremost for blame . he be deeply and sincerely affect by the calamity he have cause . alas ! he be only an instrument . your poor aunt be utterly prostrate and talk strange thing of her daughter 's death . she be only happy in drudge . Dr. Bairam say we must under any circumstance keep she employ . whilst she be do something , she can chat freely , but the moment her hand be not occupy she give I an idea that she be go into a fit . 
 " we expect the dear child 's uncle to - day . Mr. Thompson be here . I have take he upstairs to look at she . that poor young man have a true heart . 
 " come at once . you will not be in time to see she . she will lie at Raynham . if you could you would see an angel . he sit by her side for hour . I can give you no description of her beauty . 
 " you will not delay , I know , dear Austin , and I want you , for your presence will make I more charitable than I find it possible to be . have you notice the expression in the eye of blind man ? that be just how Richard look , as he lie there silent in his bed strive to image she on his brain .
